<td class="hlist" colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><a href="/wiki/Australia_at_the_1906_Intercalated_Games" title="Australia at the 1906 Intercalated Games">1906</a> Intercalated Games<br/>
<img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="1000" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Flag_of_Australasian_team_for_Olympic_games.svg/23px-Flag_of_Australasian_team_for_Olympic_games.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Flag_of_Australasian_team_for_Olympic_games.svg/35px-Flag_of_Australasian_team_for_Olympic_games.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Flag_of_Australasian_team_for_Olympic_games.svg/46px-Flag_of_Australasian_team_for_Olympic_games.svg.png 2x" width="23"/>Â <a href="/wiki/Australasia_at_the_Olympics" title="Australasia at the Olympics">Australasia</a> (1908â1912)</td>

<p><b>Australia</b> was the host nation for the <b><a href="/wiki/2000_Summer_Olympics" title="2000 Summer Olympics">2000 Summer Olympics</a></b> in <a href="/wiki/Sydney" title="Sydney">Sydney</a>. Australian athletes have competed in every <a href="/wiki/Summer_Olympic_Games" title="Summer Olympic Games">Summer Olympic Games</a>. 628 competitors, 341 men and 276 women, took part in 270 events in 34 sports.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sports-reference_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-sports-reference-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Archery">Archery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Australia_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Archery">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Archery_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics" title="Archery at the 2000 Summer Olympics">Archery at the 2000 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Australia won its first Olympic gold medal in the sport of archery in <a href="/wiki/Sydney" title="Sydney">Sydney</a>. <a href="/wiki/Simon_Fairweather" title="Simon Fairweather">Simon Fairweather</a> defeated all six archers he faced, including a comfortable seven-point victory in the final.</p>

<dt><small>Key</small></dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><small><b>Note</b>âRanks given for track events are within the athlete's heat only</small></li>
<li><small><b>Q</b> = Qualified for the next round</small></li>
<li><small><b>q</b> = Qualified for the next round as a fastest loser <i>or</i>, in field events, by position without achieving the qualifying target</small></li>
<li><small><b>NR</b> = National record</small></li>
<li><small>N/A = Round not applicable for the event</small></li>
<li><small>Bye = Athlete not required to compete in round</small></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Baseball">Baseball</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Australia_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Baseball">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Baseball_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics" title="Baseball at the 2000 Summer Olympics">Baseball at the 2000 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Men.27s_Team_Competition">Men's Team Competition</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Australia_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Men's Team Competition">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Australians' second appearance in the Olympic baseball tournament resulted in the team moving up one place in the rankings, from seventh to sixth. They defeated <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Korea_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics" title="Korea at the 2000 Summer Olympics">Korea</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Africa_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics" title="South Africa at the 2000 Summer Olympics">South Africa</a> but lost to the five other teams in competition to finish outside the top four and find themselves eliminated after the preliminaries.</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Preliminary Round Robin</b>
<ul>
<li>Lost to Netherlands (4-6)</li>
<li>Defeated Korea (5-3)</li>
<li>Lost to Japan (3-7)</li>
<li>Defeated South Africa (10-4)</li>
<li>Lost to Cuba (0-1)</li>
<li>Lost to Italy (7-8)</li>
<li>Lost to United States (1-12) â did not advance</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><b>Team Roster</b>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sailing">Sailing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Australia_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Sailing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Sailing_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics" title="Sailing at the 2000 Summer Olympics">Sailing at the 2000 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Australia competed in all of the sailing events at the 2000 Olympics. They won 2 golds, 1 silver and 1 bronze.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Swimming">Swimming</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Australia_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Swimming">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Swimming_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics" title="Swimming at the 2000 Summer Olympics">Swimming at the 2000 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Australia was very successful in the swimming venue at the 2000 Olympics. They won 5 Gold, 9 Silver, and 4 Bronze medals. The biggest rivalry, both in the press and in the pool, was between the United States and Australia relay teams. In the 4 Ã 100 m relay, the Americans had won the event every time it had been contested. Australia was able to edge out the Americans by .19 seconds to win the gold medal. The Australians also set three world records. The 2000 Olympics also saw the emergence of <a href="/wiki/Ian_Thorpe" title="Ian Thorpe">Ian Thorpe</a> as an Olympic champion in the Men's 400 m Freestyle.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Women.27s_Team_Competition_7">Women's Team Competition</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Australia_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Women's Team Competition">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
